  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_d289fb82-6306-4dba-95ce-d9f808b75408'
      });

<span id="freeTextContainer16771595016562692744">Livie has always been the stable one of the two Cleary sisters, handling her parents' tragic death and Kacey's self-destructive phase with strength and maturity. But underneath that exterior is a little girl hanging onto the last words her father ever spoke to her. “Make me proud,” he had said. She promised she would...and she’s done her best over the past seven years with</span>
  <span id="freeText16771595016562692744" style="display:none">Livie has always been the stable one of the two Cleary sisters, handling her parents' tragic death and Kacey's self-destructive phase with strength and maturity. But underneath that exterior is a little girl hanging onto the last words her father ever spoke to her. “Make me proud,” he had said. She promised she would...and she’s done her best over the past seven years with every choice, with every word, with every action.<br /><br />Livie walks into Princeton with a solid plan, and she’s dead set on delivering on it: Rock her classes, set herself up for medical school, and meet a good, respectable guy that she’s going to someday marry. What isn’t part of her plan are Jell-O shots, a lovable, party animal roommate she can’t say ‘no’ to, and Ashton, the gorgeous captain of the men’s rowing team. Definitely him. He’s an arrogant ass who makes Livie’s usually non-existent temper flare and everything she doesn’t want in a guy. Worse, he’s best friends and roommates with Connor, who happens to fits Livie’s criteria perfectly. So why does she keep thinking about Ashton?<br /><br />As Livie finds herself facing mediocre grades, career aspirations she no longer thinks she can handle, and feelings for Ashton that she shouldn’t have, she’s forced to let go of her last promise to her father and, with it, the only identity that she knows.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16771595016562692744" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

However, you do not need to read "Ten Tiny Breaths" to understand "One Tiny Lie " 's story.<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>

<div id="review_476040300" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/476040300" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/476040300?book_show_action=true">Dec 12, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer476040300" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1872371821040421706"><i>One Tiny Lie</i> was nothing like I expected it to be. I think it should have been called <i>One Giant Clusterf*ck.</i> There were parts I genuinely LOVED, parts I HATED, but overall, the book just really stressed me out. My anxiety level was through the roof. Just think of it like this- If <u>Ten Tiny Breaths </u>and <u>Thoughtless</u> had a love child, this would be it. I was so conflicted on how to rate this one... I spent two whole days thinking about it. I thought 4, then 3, then 5... I am going with <b>5 Stars</b> Why yo</span>
  <span id="freeText1872371821040421706" style="display:none"><i>One Tiny Lie</i> was nothing like I expected it to be. I think it should have been called <i>One Giant Clusterf*ck.</i> There were parts I genuinely LOVED, parts I HATED, but overall, the book just really stressed me out. My anxiety level was through the roof. Just think of it like this- If <u>Ten Tiny Breaths </u>and <u>Thoughtless</u> had a love child, this would be it. I was so conflicted on how to rate this one... I spent two whole days thinking about it. I thought 4, then 3, then 5... I am going with <b>5 Stars</b> Why you ask, when it was a giant clusterf*ck? Well- the main issue I had with the book was <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The REPETITIVE CHEATING!!!! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, and Thoughtless had the same thing going on. And in Thoughtless, the heroine was WAY more annoying, it got 5 stars, so yeah... thats my justification lol! I loved Livie, I LOVED Ash, and the writing was brilliant so a 5 star read for me! One of the main points of this story was that Livie doesn't have to be <b>perfect</b>, trust me, she wasn't! But I still loved her and this book! Now that you have read my mini-rant... On to the review!!! <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/a286ea5f-77c8-44f9-b97c-c06c97eb3925_zpsab36c568.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400637i/776707.jpg" alt=" photo a286ea5f-77c8-44f9-b97c-c06c97eb3925_zpsab36c568.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>Ten Tiny Breaths</i> was one of my favorite reads of 2012. It was just fantastic. If you haven’t read it, I HIGHLY recommend it. One of the main reasons I loved it so much was the main character’s little sister, Livie. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/21736b23-95cc-4e6e-bdf6-5b91ecafc67b_zps92133d9d.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400637i/776708.jpg" alt=" photo 21736b23-95cc-4e6e-bdf6-5b91ecafc67b_zps92133d9d.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>“You’re too perfect, Livie.”</i><br><br>Livie is not so little anymore. She is getting ready to start her freshmen year at college, Princeton to be exact. Where she has always planned on going. Livie has every thing planned out. She is as close to perfect as they come. A straight ‘A’ student, never gets in trouble, doesn’t drink, smoke, mess around with guys... she is on the straight and narrow. But all of that is about to change. And it’s dr’s orders. Dr. Stayner and Kacey both agree that Livie needs to loosen up, have some fun, find herself. She is just too perfect and she is about to crack. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/17759fe2-8c44-4b6f-a79a-0aa2611218b6_zpsdd6d6d09.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400637i/776709.jpg" alt=" photo 17759fe2-8c44-4b6f-a79a-0aa2611218b6_zpsdd6d6d09.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“You are one of the kindest souls I’ve ever met, Livie. You respond to human heartache so acutely. It’s like you absorb other’s pain. Despite your extreme shyness, you will do just about anything not to fail. It’s time to find out who you really are.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/ONeTinyLIe-perfect_zps07f3727e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400637i/776710.jpg" alt=" photo ONeTinyLIe-perfect_zps07f3727e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Her first night at Princeton changes everything. Kacey takes her, unwillingly, to a college party. She indulges with many jello shots, and she meets Ash. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/53bc9479-1df4-4e3c-972f-5cc67e1e90fe_zps7d2d96de.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400637i/776711._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 53bc9479-1df4-4e3c-972f-5cc67e1e90fe_zps7d2d96de.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“And he’s pretty much the hottest guy at this school. And also a giant ass. And a bit of a man whore.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b> I pretty much loved Ash from the start. He’s a jerk, an ass, a man whore, and just perfect. Except for one little thing... he has a girlfriend. Livie finds out about that only after she spends the evening drunk and wild with him. She tries to avoid him at all costs, even meets someone else. Connor. Connor is a nice guy. Just the type of guy she SHOULD be dating, but there is something missing there. He’s not Ashton. Ashton and Connor are best friends, things get complicated. The more time Livie spends with Ash, the more she learns about him. She see’s the real him. At least the parts he will let her see. Ashton doesn’t have the perfect easy going life he shows to the outside. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/095b13ea-b3b7-4b86-8c7f-9ce0089c2e4c_zpsce56760f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400637i/776712.jpg" alt=" photo 095b13ea-b3b7-4b86-8c7f-9ce0089c2e4c_zpsce56760f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Ash wants Livie, but he needs to stay with his girl, for reasons you don’t yet know. Let me just say, as much as I loved Ashton, he is the KING OF MIXED SIGNALS!!!! Tell someone to stay away from you, that she is better off with Connor, then you give her notes like this: <br><b>1- I’m brilliant<br>2- I’m charming<br>3- I’m hung like a thoroughbred<br>4- I’ve stopped all philandering<br>5- I’m highly skilled, as you’ve learned the other night<br>P.S. Stop staring at my hands. I know what you want me to do with them.</b> <br>Confusing, right???? Livie wants to end it with Connor, she wants to be with Ash, but its complicated. Ashton has reasons for the things that he does. Reasons for pushing Livie away. If he could be with her, he would.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/OneTinyLIe-love_zpsede5568f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400637i/776713.jpg" alt=" photo OneTinyLIe-love_zpsede5568f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <blockquote>Life’s all about trial and error.</blockquote>
</b><br>My biggest issue with the book, and I’m sure many would agree:  <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Ash and Livie hooked up so much in this book, and she never broke it off with Connor. I mean WTF?!?!?! That is just not cool! I understand why Ash is with his girl, I guess- but there was no reason to drag Connor along. She should have broken up with him long before she was messing around with Ash, and especially before she SLEPT WITH ASH, with Connor just downstairs!!! Really lady? Okay- end of rant for now ;D  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/5804c7e0-a0c4-4385-8413-6ff7e882b2e3_zps0a932ad8.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400637i/776714.jpg" alt=" photo 5804c7e0-a0c4-4385-8413-6ff7e882b2e3_zps0a932ad8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>It’s undeniable that Ashton and Livie have something special. She sees a part of him that no one else does, and he shows her that its okay to not be perfect. But with all the complications, will this One Tiny Lie make everything around them crumble?<br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Irish, if there’s one thing I’ve never been able to forget, it’s a single second with you.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>I laughed, I cried, I was stressed out to the MAX. It was great catching up with the old crew. Kacey, Trent, Storm, Dr. Stayner. Livie wasn’t perfect, but I think that was THE POINT of the book. It’s okay to make mistakes, screw up, change your mind. Life goes on. And you all know<u> I fell in love with</u><b> Ashton.</b> Come on, the boy is <b>damaged,</b> and he is a <b>jerk</b>, with a side of <b>man whore</b>. What is not to love??? I am glad we got to the bottom of what was going on with him, it made me feel better. Enjoyed the ending. <br><br>K.A. Tucker’s writing is marvelous. This woman has a way with words. If you enjoyed <i>Ten Tiny Breaths</i>, and you don’t mind some crazy angst, a love triangle, with a side of anxiety, check this one out! If you can’t handle any of the above, it may not be for you. With all that said, it wasn’t perfect, the main characters were flawed, but THAT’S THE POINT! I still loved it and it gets 5 stars from this reader!!!!!<br><br><i>*ARC provided by Atria Books via Netgalley in exchange for an honest review*</i><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="1872371821040421706" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_487669128" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/487669128" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/487669128?book_show_action=true">Dec 28, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer487669128" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13356371158343131071"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402358i/781986._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> I love this book!!! 4.5 stars <br/><br/>If you loved Ten Tiny Breaths, you'll love this one too! It was different in many ways and definitely stood on it's own but it had that same spark! I just could not put it down! </b><br/><br/>I have to say this story really surprised me. It went in a really different direction than I was expecting and I just LOVED that about it! See, it was actually a bit of a forbidden romance. Here's the set up:<br/><br/>Livie was always mature for her age and after the tragedies her family suffered thr</span>
  <span id="freeText13356371158343131071" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402358i/781986._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> I love this book!!! 4.5 stars <br><br>If you loved Ten Tiny Breaths, you'll love this one too! It was different in many ways and definitely stood on it's own but it had that same spark! I just could not put it down! </b><br><br>I have to say this story really surprised me. It went in a really different direction than I was expecting and I just LOVED that about it! See, it was actually a bit of a forbidden romance. Here's the set up:<br><br>Livie was always mature for her age and after the tragedies her family suffered through, she grew up too fast too soon. Her shrink just wanted her to to let loose and LIVE a little and so her sister, Kasey, takes her out partying. She wakes up the next day with very fuzzy memories, a brand new tattoo on her back and in a room full of people, one of whom happens to be Ashton.<br><br>To her horror, Ashton seems to remember everything but... seems more than happy to forget it. Much to her disappointment. At this point, she meets his best friend Connor who is pretty much perfect, gorgeous, Irish and totally the kind of guy she could see herself with while Ashton is gorgeous, mysterious, but more than a bit of a man-whore and is hiding something underneath it all. But even with this perfect guy in front of her, she can't stop thinking about the one who shouldn't be on her mind.... Ashton.<br><br><i> <blockquote> "... you're not a fuck-buddy kind of girl and he's not boyfriend material. Clearly." </blockquote> </i> <br>As the story goes on, Ashton keeps insisting that they shouldn't be together, that he isn't good for her... and something about it makes her wonder if there's more to his story than meets the eye.<br><br><i> <b> <blockquote> "Why?"<br>"He looks away for a minute and I watch his jaw clench... "Because you're not a one-night-stand girl, Irish." Leaning in to place a kiss on my jawline, he whispers. "You're my forever girl." </blockquote> </b></i> <br>Ashton was just the kind of hero I love. Broken/tortured heroes just break my heart in a way that just makes me fall even harder for them and Ashton was definitely one of those characters. Between that and just his whole attitude and all the swoony and sweet things he did, I found it impossible not to fall in love with him.<br><br>It was all about the little things... flirty comments, a glance that has so much meaning, a little touch that lingers too long, a glimpse into something deeper behind the carefree exterior.<br><br>But I have to say that when his back story came out, it seriously just made my heart hurt. It's bad, guys. Really bad. I was trying to think and figure out what exactly his reasons could be for staying away but nothing that I came up with made sense. But when the reason was brought out into the open, it totally and completely explained EVERYTHING. It was very well put together, took me by surprise and ended up being fully believable given the context of the story.<br><br>As for Livie, I really liked watching her journey as she figured out what she wanted most out of her life. Up until now, she'd always taken the safe road. The right road. Connor was safe, right, perfect. And Ashton wasn't. This story was about her letting go, learning to live, and learning to choose with her heart over her head.<br><br><i> <blockquote> "Life has a funny way of creating it's own tests. It throws curve balls that make you do and think and feel things that are in direct conflict with what you had planned and don't allow you to operate in terms of black and white." </blockquote></i> <br>I loved watching Livie and Ashton dance around each other a bit in the beginning. The reason I called this a forbidden romance is that there were genuine reasons why they couldn't be together at first and so everything between then was in these little, emotionally charged stolen moments.<br><br>I'm not usually a fan of love triangles but the reason I was totally okay with this book was that you could tell right from the start that Livie and Ashton were right for each other. There was really no question there. It was just a matter of figuring out how they'd end up together.<br><br>The entire book was really well-written but I also have to say that the scene where Livie figured out what had happened to Ash in his past was just phenomenal. I felt like I discovered it right alone with her and came to the realization at the same moment that she did. That moment? Omg I was just right THERE. I teared up, got chills. It was really emotional and I loved it.<br><br>The story wasn't a fast build but I enjoyed the pacing. Around 50% in, my heart really started to race as the layers built. The detailing and character development was so engaging that honestly I just wanted to read this in one sitting. Add that to the fact that broken/tortured heroes are just my all-time favorite and really this book just hit all the right marks with me. I cared, really CARED about the characters and the story.<br><br>There is definitely steam in this book but it's very tastefully written and not graphic. But trust me, you'll feel it!<br><br>I also loved that we got to see quite a bit of Kasey and Trent in this. I think it's wonderful when, in sequels, the characters from the first book are remembered and included. It gives the whole story a really wonderful, well-rounded feeling.<br><br>Oh and yes, there is a happy ending! Fully resolved, no cliffhanger!<br><br>I love the whole interconnected sort of family network that has been built between this book and the first one. I've heard that the next book will be about Cain (he's so mysterious! I want to know more!) and then Ben. I really can't wait!!<br><br>Each of the books in this series can technically be read as stand alones but I do suggest reading them in order if you can.<br><br>I highly recommend this series!<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402358i/781987._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>BLURB --&gt; <i> <br>Livie has always been the stable one of the two Cleary sisters, handling her parents' tragic death and Kacey's self-destructive phase with strength and maturity. But underneath that exterior is a little girl hanging onto the last words her father ever spoke to her. “Make me proud,” he had said. She promised she would...and she’s done her best over the past seven years with every choice, with every word, with every action.<br><br>Livie walks into Princeton with a solid plan, and she’s dead set on delivering on it: Rock her classes, set herself up for medical school, and meet a good, respectable guy that she’s going to someday marry. What isn’t part of her plan are Jell-O shots, a lovable, party animal roommate she can’t say ‘no’ to, and Ashton, the gorgeous captain of the men’s rowing team. Definitely him. He’s an arrogant ass who makes Livie’s usually non-existent temper flare and everything she doesn’t want in a guy. Worse, he’s best friends and roommates with Connor, who happens to fits Livie’s criteria perfectly. So why does she keep thinking about Ashton?<br><br>As Livie finds herself facing mediocre grades, career aspirations she no longer thinks she can handle, and feelings for Ashton that she shouldn’t have, she’s forced to let go of her last promise to her father and, with it, the only identity that she knows. </i><br><br><br><b> For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="13356371158343131071" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Pearl Angeli" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31514572-pearl-angeli"><img alt="Pearl Angeli" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1588420465p2/31514572.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1741192675?book_show_action=true">Aug 28, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pearl Angeli" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pearl Angeli" href="/user/show/31514572-pearl-angeli">Pearl Angeli</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781476740478" href="/book/show/17571724-one-tiny-lie">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=cute-book-couple">cute-book-couple</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=2016-reads">2016-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=damn-this-guy-is-perfect">damn-this-guy-is-perfect</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=hot-male-characters">hot-male-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=owned-physical-copy">owned-physical-copy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=angst-overload">angst-overload</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=new-adult-contemporary">new-adult-contemporary</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1741192675" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3505410877366038816"><b>3 Stars!</b><br/><br/>This book is all about <b>Livie Cleary</b>, the sister of <b>Kacey Cleary</b> from Ten Tiny Breaths. Unlike her sister, she grew up with a different outlook in life. She's intellectual and so much in control with everything. When she went to <i>Princeton University</i> to pursue her childhood dream of becoming a pediatrician, her meek and virginal lifestyle changed. She was introduced to lots of college drunken parties which were new to her. The first time she was exposed to a party, she met the gorgeous col</span>
  <span id="freeText3505410877366038816" style="display:none"><b>3 Stars!</b><br><br>This book is all about <b>Livie Cleary</b>, the sister of <b>Kacey Cleary</b> from Ten Tiny Breaths. Unlike her sister, she grew up with a different outlook in life. She's intellectual and so much in control with everything. When she went to <i>Princeton University</i> to pursue her childhood dream of becoming a pediatrician, her meek and virginal lifestyle changed. She was introduced to lots of college drunken parties which were new to her. The first time she was exposed to a party, she met the gorgeous college manwhore <b>Ashton Henley</b> and had an unforgettable one night hook-up with him. There's certainly an attraction going on between them. But when she met Irishman <b>Connor</b>, she decided that he's the right one for her because he is different compared to Ashton. Connor is the exact opposite and he's uncomplicated. But of course she soon realized that she's more attracted to Ashton because of their undeniable sexual tension whenever they see each other.<br><br>There was certainly an <b>angst</b> in this book. It wasn't a normal college romance book where majority falls into the flirty side. This one dealt with certain issues but it wasn't as heavy as Ten Tiny Breaths.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Because you’re not a one-night girl, Irish. You’re my forever girl."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>The problem I had with this book was the heroine. I have nothing against Livie. I think she's a good and likable character. I just didn't really connect with her POV and her giggles and blushes that she always did in this book. Her mannerisms were kind of annoying. Sometimes she also overreacts to certain things and over-analyze them and it made me face palm myself at least a couple of times.<br><br>The thing that I loved here, though, was Ashton. One with a playful charm but with deep issues underneath the amused smiles, he's the kind of male lead that interests me. I've always rooted for him since the first time he was introduced in the book.<br><br>The romance was good and there were delightfully sexy times, too. I loved that the author delved into a different theme this time. I have always been a sucker for college romance books and the college air in this story was something that drew me in. Yes, there was a little bit of love triangle that happened but it was obvious who's the love interest here.<br><br>I found the story, as a whole, okay but it didn't capture me like I would have hoped. There wasn't really something that's remarkable and special in this book. I must say I enjoyed Ten Tiny Breaths more because of the amazing storyline that came with a perfect, mind-blowing plot twist. Still, One Tiny Lie wasn't a bad read. I'm looking forward to enjoying the rest of the series more.<br><br><blockquote>
  <p>
    <a href="https://pagesofpearl.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
      <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472382775i/20186886._SX540_.jpg" alt="Pages of Pearl" width="400" height="150" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
    </a>
  </p>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1464648592i/19260109.png" width="250" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_1174435231" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1174435231" />
    <a title="Ramona Popescu " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/33526516-ramona-popescu"><img alt="Ramona Popescu " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594649997p2/33526516.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1174435231?book_show_action=true">Jan 20, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ramona Popescu " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ramona Popescu " href="/user/show/33526516-ramona-popescu">Ramona Popescu </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=sweet-as-sugar">sweet-as-sugar</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1174435231" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2064868410695535126">After reading Ten Tiny Breaths I became a fan of K.A.Tucker mainly because of the message she sends to readers. I always enjoyed a book with a strong message, that raises awareness of a social problem and managed to make you reconsider about certain ideas you may had and thought they were correct. <br/><br/>The one important thing that reading thought me was not to judge, to look deeper into someone's personality and try to identify what makes them click and act that way. And there are a lot of books that</span>
  <span id="freeText2064868410695535126" style="display:none">After reading Ten Tiny Breaths I became a fan of K.A.Tucker mainly because of the message she sends to readers. I always enjoyed a book with a strong message, that raises awareness of a social problem and managed to make you reconsider about certain ideas you may had and thought they were correct. <br><br>The one important thing that reading thought me was not to judge, to look deeper into someone's personality and try to identify what makes them click and act that way. And there are a lot of books that simply give you reality on a plate, making you discover that underneath the exterior comes a great story.<br><br>I learned that with Kacey and I was convinced that with Livie it will be the same experience. The story chicks off 3 years after Ten Tiny Breaths, when Livie is 18 and ready to go to Princeton. Yes, our little sister has grown up into a beautiful lady, smarter and more determined to follow her father's footsteps. The only problem with our dear girl is that she is so focused on pleasing others that she forgot to live for herself. Her life is kind of boring, without fun or extra activities, making her kind of geeky. So, Kacey decides to celebrate her baby sister going to Princeton and have some fun, just the 2 of them. We all know Kacey's wild side and there are no surprises something unforgettable will happen that night. At that party, Livie meets Ashton, a gorgeous guy who surprises her with his witty, charming and egomaniac personality. What happens that night will be a crazy chain of events, that will lead Livie and Ashton closer, although their relationship will initially be cat and mouse like. But you know what they say, opposites attract and this 2 are living proof. <br><br>So, a very delicious beginning for our dear couple, but once you really get the feel of the story, it will get better. Certain problems occur, like Ashton's girlfriend or Connor, Ashton's best friend, who will date Livie, but that just adds the salt and pepper to our story. As you know from Ten Tiny Breaths, not everything is what it seems and there will be motives behind our character's behavior. You just have to be patient enough to discover them and remember not to judge.<br><br>I loved Livie from the very first word I read about her in Ten Tiny Breaths. I liked the way she stood by her sister, cared for her, making her the center of her universe. They only had each other and this connection was overwhelming for me. But nobody actually thought much about Livie when Kacey had that accident. All focus was on Kacey because she actually lived it, but what about her sister? She suffered a terrible lost too and not to mention that she had to witness every day the destructive path Kacey was taking. The breakdown she had in the hospital in Ten Tiny Breaths only indicated the suffering and hurt she felt and it was only a matter of time until she would break. I liked that she was so innocent, the kind of sweet innocence that made you want to hug her and be there for her.<br><br>Ashton was exactly the guy she needed to get her out of her comfort zone. But, they were alike in so many ways, because they had hidden many feelings inside and it was hard to figure after a while what was true and what was pretending. I liked him as a hero, despite that he kept on telling Livie he was not OK for her. He knew exactly what he was getting himself into, but at a certain point he didn't care, because it is impossible to resist Livie. Although he was the one to push her away, he also pulled her in many times, and it kind of confused me at times. Adding Connor in the equation was exciting, because this was the perfect example that life is not all the times meant to be lived by rules and fixed ideas. Livie thought the perfect guy for her has to be sweet, respectful, cute and nice, and she ended up falling in love with the complicated but gorgeous bad boy. How about that? This was a perfect way of her growing up, realizing things and taking decision for her own well, not for the acceptance of others. She managed after meeting Asthon to take chances, and although she suffered a lot, she also gained a lot, that made her more stronger and independent. <br><br>So this was a sweet story about 2 different persons who realize they have a lot in common and as a bonus, K.A.Tucker managed once more to insert a strong social message that made me cry a little because of its intensity and frequency in families around the world.<br><br>4 stars!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479123324i/21149668._SX540_.png" width="500" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For more reviews please check <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://readwithloveblog.wordpress.com">https://readwithloveblog.wordpress.com</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="2064868410695535126" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer15873142071248359968">I've always wanted to read this when I accidentally saw a picture quote few weeks ago and I totally don't regret doing so.<br/><br/>It's another beautiful story between two teenagers, Livie and Ashton. Both of them experienced something that left scars deeply inside their hearts, but what I liked most is the fact that this time, it was the <b>male character</b> who'd been abused instead of the female. I don't know why, but there are way too many similar stories that always described the young ladies as someone e</span>
  <span id="freeText15873142071248359968" style="display:none">I've always wanted to read this when I accidentally saw a picture quote few weeks ago and I totally don't regret doing so.<br /><br />It's another beautiful story between two teenagers, Livie and Ashton. Both of them experienced something that left scars deeply inside their hearts, but what I liked most is the fact that this time, it was the <b>male character</b> who'd been abused instead of the female. I don't know why, but there are way too many similar stories that always described the young ladies as someone entirely broken or too vulnerable to live their lives, and I'm glad it isn't what's going on with this book.<br /><br />Since I simply skimmed through the book within several hours, all I can say is that <b>the ending was the BEST part of the story</b>. The author kind of threw out many questions about Ashton to keep the readers wondering the truth behind them and he never gave a complete answer to them, so it's pure perfection that he did spill them out eventually. <i>That</i> was really something worth waiting for and made this book more valuable. :)<br /><br />Last but not least, thanks to my great friend, Jasmin, for recommending this one. I know it's been awhile since you finished this, but thanks so much for bringing another satisfying NA novel in my reading life. :&gt;</span>

<div id="review_544430634" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/544430634" />
    <a title="Vikki ~ *squee* lite ~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3758447-vikki-squee-lite"><img alt="Vikki ~ *squee* lite ~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1368215503p2/3758447.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/544430634?book_show_action=true">Feb 23, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Vikki ~ *squee* lite ~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Vikki ~ *squee* lite ~" href="/user/show/3758447-vikki-squee-lite">Vikki ~ *squee* lite ~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3758447-vikki-squee-lite?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3758447-vikki-squee-lite?shelf=need-to-review">need-to-review</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer544430634" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4121193368255258120">Disclaimers: This is probably going to be more rant then review. This book sent my blood pressure skyrocketing. I was cursing at the characters, I wanted to slap a couple of people and shake the heck out of Livie more than once. <br/><br/>I have to start off saying I loved Ten Tiny Breaths. I mean I LOVED it. It's one of my top books of last year. One of the big reasons I loved it? Livie. She was a fantastic character. I adored everything about her, and I could not have been more thrilled for her to get h</span>
  <span id="freeText4121193368255258120" style="display:none">Disclaimers: This is probably going to be more rant then review. This book sent my blood pressure skyrocketing. I was cursing at the characters, I wanted to slap a couple of people and shake the heck out of Livie more than once. <br /><br />I have to start off saying I loved Ten Tiny Breaths. I mean I LOVED it. It's one of my top books of last year. One of the big reasons I loved it? Livie. She was a fantastic character. I adored everything about her, and I could not have been more thrilled for her to get her own book. So, saying my expectations where high is putting it mildly. <br /><br />I also need to disclose that cheating is a HUGE no-no for me (in real and book life :). It can ruin a good book for me faster than any insta-love or triangle. <br /><br />Ok, on to the review ....<br /><br />I'm going to attempt to do this without putting forth any untagged spoilers. This could be a problem, since my issues were plot related, and not "writing" related, but I'm going to do my best to keep it generic. <b> *and note my tagged spoilers, are REAL spoilers, so don't click unless you really want to know *. Seriously, I'm not kidding, don't do it! </b> <br /><br />The book opens with Livie getting ready to head off to Princeton. Kacey is sure that Livie is just "too good" and is on the verge of "cracking" so she spends the summer talking to Dr. Stayner. He does his best to bring her out of her shell by getting her to perform tasks over the summer to take her out of her comfort zone. <br /><br />The whole idea was to get her to think outside of the life she has had planned for herself since she was nine. To try and get her to realize she doesn't have to be perfect. Well, I think it worked, because she gets to college, and "perfect" gets left so far in the dust you can't even see it anymore. <br /><br />The first time she meets Ashton is at an off campus party, before classes start. Kacey is there, and she is encouraging her (with Dr. Stayner's approval) to get drunk, and perhaps even get "under" someone. (Please do not get me started about this guys methods of therapy. I know this is a book,and he's supposed to be "unconventional" , but the dude would have lost his license so fast in real life it's not even funny). <br /><br />They don't do the nasty, but they do hook up. The next day he asks her to keep it quite, and tells her he regrets doing it. Yeah, OUCH. So begins the push pull that characterizes the entire novel. Ashton pursues her - seeks her out, says something sweet, maybe starts the seduction, and Livie, she falls for it, only for him to turn around and squash her like a bug. Every.single.time. <br /><br />She eventually meets Connor (who happens to be Ashton's best friend). This doesn't stop the cycle. Hell, it makes it worse, oh so much worse, because we get to add layers of guilt along with the nice little mind-fuck. <br /><br />You slowly learn that there is a reason that Ashton keeps pushing her away. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ the first seems to be his long distance, long term girlfriend - yes folks, we have all kinds of cheating going on - then we learn its way bigger than that  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> And, I get it. I get why he had to keep up his current life. At the same time, it doesn't change my feelings that he was a selfish bastard for continuing to string Livie along when he had NO intention of changing anything. I'm sympathetic to his predicament, but it's not enough for me to forgive him.<br /><br />I think, maybe, I could have forgiven Ashton, until the Halloween party, but after that, there was no coming back for me. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ the fact that he slept with Livie - took her virginity, after getting ENGAGED to Diana, when he had NO intention of breaking it off with her was just too much for me. I was done with him.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br /><br /><br />I was also horribly disappointed in Livie. I tried to give her a pass because she was just so darn inexperienced, but Connor is a nice guy. There was no reason to string him along <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ it was bad enough she was helping Ashton cheat on Diana  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> It wasn't even like she was really torn between the two of them - there was no point in continuing to date Connor. <br /><br />The ending felt rushed to me. We tied out all the lose ends (with some very... unrealistic intervention of some other characters) at warp speed. All the sudden everything was ok. It didn't feel real to me. The epilogue was nice, but it didn't give me enough warm and fuzzies to overcome all the nasty that came before it. <br /><br />Now, to be fair, the book is not all bad. I liked that Livie does learn to forge her own path. Ashton was, despite his flaws, hot as all hell, and had some seriously swoon-worthy lines. I loved seeing Kacey, Trent, Ben and Cain again. (I really want a Cain book!!!). The whole thing was certainly emotionally engaging (even if my emotions were mostly rage and frustration). <br /><br />However, none of that was enough to get me past my sticking points. I still think that K.A. Tucker is a fantastic author. I'll be first in line to preorder whatever her next book is, but this one just wasn't for me. <br /><br /><i> ARC provided by Atria books via NetGalley </i> </span>
  <a data-text-id="4121193368255258120" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_633047367" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/633047367" />
    <a title="Heather K (dentist in my spare time)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time"><img alt="Heather K (dentist in my spare time)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1365526640p2/13070326.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/633047367?book_show_action=true">Jun 04, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Heather K (dentist in my spare time)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Heather K (dentist in my spare time)" href="/user/show/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time">Heather K (dentist in my spare time)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=full-of-angst">full-of-angst</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=mixed-emotions">mixed-emotions</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=hype-hype-hype">hype-hype-hype</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=m-f">m-f</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=net-galley">net-galley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=losing-the-v-card">losing-the-v-card</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=hot-hot-hot">hot-hot-hot</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer633047367" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7479336568034645853">**2.5 stars**<br/> <br/><b>Cheater, cheater pumpkin eater! Livie, you disappoint me.</b><br/><br/>I was in the camp that liked <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15990969.Ten_Tiny_Breaths__Ten_Tiny_Breaths___1_' title='Ten Tiny Breaths (Ten Tiny Breaths, #1) by K.A. Tucker' rel='nofollow noopener'>Ten Tiny Breaths</a>. I excused Trent's stalker behavior, and I just sat back and enjoyed the chemistry between Trent and Kasey. When I heard that Livie was getting her own book to tell her story, I was pretty excited. I expected this book to be great and went into it with high hopes. It had a beautiful cover and a lot of hype- what could go wrong?! And for the first 50% or so, I really enjoyed "One T</span>
  <span id="freeText7479336568034645853" style="display:none">**2.5 stars**<br /> <br /><b>Cheater, cheater pumpkin eater! Livie, you disappoint me.</b><br /><br />I was in the camp that liked <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15990969.Ten_Tiny_Breaths__Ten_Tiny_Breaths___1_" title="Ten Tiny Breaths (Ten Tiny Breaths, #1) by K.A. Tucker" rel="nofollow noopener">Ten Tiny Breaths</a>. I excused Trent's stalker behavior, and I just sat back and enjoyed the chemistry between Trent and Kasey. When I heard that Livie was getting her own book to tell her story, I was pretty excited. I expected this book to be great and went into it with high hopes. It had a beautiful cover and a lot of hype- what could go wrong?! And for the first 50% or so, I really enjoyed "One Tiny Lie". However, soon after it took a turn for the worst and I dropped my star-rating like a hot potato. <br /><br />Livie enters her freshman year at Princeton feeling the pressure to be perfect. She wants to make her deceased parents proud and so she is determined to study hard so she can go on and be the pediatric oncologist that they always wanted her to be. However, at her first college party, with the influence of Kasey (naughty sister!), she gets wasted and makes out with the very hot captain of the crew team, Ashton. Though she feels chemistry between them, Livie decides that Ashton isn't boyfriend material and tries to move on with a nice boy that she meets later on campus (Connor). However, avoiding Ashton and her feelings for him are not as easy as Livie originally though. <br /><br />Though I should be sick of it by now, the trope of the virginal girl and the bad boy player still has some draw for me. I don't mind reading about how the good girl changes a player's ways. However, this isn't quite what this book is about. It is more about Livie's inability to make a decision and grow a pair. <br /><br />I am not a girl who can't read about cheating. I don't mind a little cheating in books as long as it is nipped in the bud early on, and the girl breaks up with the guy she was originally dating, giving him full disclosure. Full out affairs are NOT my jam. When Livie starts hooking up with Ashton as she is dating Connor, at first I excused her. However, as it progressed and Connor was used, abused, and ignored, I grew increasingly irritated with Livie. I mean, COME ON. You knew what you were doing girl, it is just bad behavior at this point. Connor was an upstanding, nice guy and I hated to see him get treated the way that Livie treated him. She honestly didn't even seem to like him at all, so stringing him along just seemed cruel. <br /><br />In addition, Livie just lets Ashton walk all over her. Each time they hooked up and he left her a little note that he didn't want to see her anymore, she never got angry. She just kind of accepted it and didn't ever bring it up to him... and they kept on hooking up! Doormat alert! I was spitting mad when <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Ashton proposed to Dana and Livie never even GOT MAD! When she saw him again, she was all like "oh, why would he think I would hate him"- come ON!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> He deserved to stew in the naughty corner for a few months at least for that one. <br /><br />However, though the cheating was a big issue for me, a bigger issue was the unbelievable character of Dr. Stayner. He did things that even the most cutting edge, experimental psychologists would never dream of doing. Starting with doing weekly therapy sessions pro bono (come on!), he did the oddest things with Livie. Popping in on her unexpectedly, encouraging dangerous behavior, and meddling HUGELY in her affairs- the stuff that he did just didn't ring true. And don't get me started on what he did at the end of the book that involved Ashton. It just went so far beyond what would be considered normal. <br /><br />Also, I think many people would be annoyed with the back and forth between Ashton and Livie. It was a constant yo-yo that gave me a headache. I didn't like all of the games between the two of them. <br /><br />To top everything off, the ending wrapped up way too neatly and quickly for my tastes. It was like conflict and angst to the Nth degree until the ending... then a buttery smooth resolution. <br /><br />I think the twist with Ashton and his parents was an interesting one (I see twists are kind of K.A. Tucker's thing), and I stayed up until 1:30 am to see what would happen in the end. However, overall this book was a bit of a disappointment. <br /><br />**Copy provided by the publisher in exchange for an honest review**</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

        <a title="Lucia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lucia" href="/user/show/8837962-lucia">Lucia</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer476043310" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16642220545885822673"><i>I could not wait for Livie's story! I loved her so much in<a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15990969.Ten_Tiny_Breaths__Ten_Tiny_Breaths___1_' title='Ten Tiny Breaths (Ten Tiny Breaths, #1) by K.A. Tucker' rel='nofollow noopener'>Ten Tiny Breaths</a> but unfortunatelly this book did not work for me.</i><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400637i/776715.png' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>This is one of the most painful reviews I have ever written. I absolutely adore K.A. Tucker's writing style an dall her previous books were 5 STARS read for me. So obviously I went to reading this book with very high expectations. However, this story contents quite intense love triangle and it truly did not sit well with me. There is no doubt that writing was superb, it wa</span>
  <span id="freeText16642220545885822673" style="display:none"><i>I could not wait for Livie's story! I loved her so much in<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15990969.Ten_Tiny_Breaths__Ten_Tiny_Breaths___1_" title="Ten Tiny Breaths (Ten Tiny Breaths, #1) by K.A. Tucker" rel="nofollow noopener">Ten Tiny Breaths</a> but unfortunatelly this book did not work for me.</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400637i/776715.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>This is one of the most painful reviews I have ever written. I absolutely adore K.A. Tucker's writing style an dall her previous books were 5 STARS read for me. So obviously I went to reading this book with very high expectations. However, this story contents quite intense love triangle and it truly did not sit well with me. There is no doubt that writing was superb, it was <b>storyline and heroine's and hero's behaviour that did not work for me</b>.<br><br>One Tiny Lie reminded me a soap opera, I just did not feel the angst of main characters and whole ending was too fairy-tale like and quite unrealistic. Saying that, I am not giving up on this author. On contrary, I cannot wait for her next book since I truly love her ideas and style of writing!<br><br><i>*ARC provided by Netgally as an exchange for honest review*</i><br><br>MORE REVIEWS ON MY BLOG <a href="http://readingismybreathing.blogspot.cz/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <b>Reading Is My Breathing</b>

<span id="freeTextContainer11208798819393234522">More reviews - > <a href='http://www.jacquelinesreads.blogspot.com' rel='nofollow noopener'>Jacqueline's Reads</a><br/><br/><b>5 STARS! Spoiler FREE Review</b> <br/><br/><a href='http://imgur.com/4ruT7CP' rel='nofollow noopener'>

  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405241i/789160.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><a href='http://imgur.com/JP11VJb' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/><b>Oh.my.word…. one word to describe <i>One Tiny Lie</i> is ONE BIG FANTASTIC YES!</b><br/><br/>Seriously people, if you haven’t picked up a KA Tucker read, you.need.to.do.it.NOW! <br/><br/>I LOVED LOVED LOVED <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/497179890' rel='nofollow noopener'> Ten Tiny Breaths</a>. <i>One Tiny Lie</i> isn’t anything like <i>Ten Tiny Breaths</i> and you would think that would upset me huh? Oh.No. Makes me love <i>One Tiny Lie</i> even more. <i>One Tiny Lie</i> is book 2 of Ten Tiny Breaths series and is a completely new and different n</span>
  <span id="freeText11208798819393234522" style="display:none">More reviews - &gt; <a href="http://www.jacquelinesreads.blogspot.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Jacqueline's Reads</a><br><br><b>5 STARS! Spoiler FREE Review</b> <br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/4ruT7CP" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405241i/789159.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/upeqtFW" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405241i/789160.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/JP11VJb" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405241i/789161.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Oh.my.word…. one word to describe <i>One Tiny Lie</i> is ONE BIG FANTASTIC YES!</b><br><br>Seriously people, if you haven’t picked up a KA Tucker read, you.need.to.do.it.NOW! <br><br>I LOVED LOVED LOVED <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/497179890" rel="nofollow noopener"> Ten Tiny Breaths</a>. <i>One Tiny Lie</i> isn’t anything like <i>Ten Tiny Breaths</i> and you would think that would upset me huh? Oh.No. Makes me love <i>One Tiny Lie</i> even more. <i>One Tiny Lie</i> is book 2 of Ten Tiny Breaths series and is a completely new and different novel from the first book BUT you still need to read <i>Ten Tiny Breaths</i> so the story isn’t ruined for you. <br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/YJEb1D4" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405241i/789162._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>[Summary]</b><br><br>Its two years later and Livie is 18, I jump for joy on this. I am happy she is legal. Anyhow, Livie is always the responsible one and has her future planned out for her. She attends her first year at Princeton and everyone wants Livie to loosen up and enjoy her college years. Livie finds this difficult, but with the help of Ashton, it might not be so difficult for Livie to be a little reckless, even though predicable, yet safe Connor seems like the obvious choice.<br><br><b>[Disclaimer]</b><br><br>If I read the blurb prior to reading, I probably wouldn’t have picked it up. I am always a little apprehensive of love triangles, it’s a difficult story line for me to get into, however, this just goes to show what a fabulous writer Tucker is, because I was hooked from page one.<br><br><b>[Livie]</b><br><br>I LOVE LOVE LOVE Livie. If Livie and I went to college together, she would be my best friend. I love Livie so much because I see myself in her. I mean, never getting anything lower than an A, oh yeah, I feel for ya girl! She’s a great Heroine. Livie is young, independent, smart, yet emotional, caring and a really great character. If you looking for a coming of age kind of character, she’s your girl. I even like that she cries so much, it’s very cute.<br><br><b>[Ashton]</b> <br><br><b>Ashton is swoon-drool-panties-down-my-leg kind of Hero.</b><br><br>Oh boy. Oh boy. Why do we “good” girls love these bad boys?! It’s just too much and I LOVE IT! <br><br><b>
  <i>I’m sure most girls do everything in their power to stage a run-in with Ashton Henley after getting drunk and making out with him on a random street corner.<br><br>But I am not most girls</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/SQUkfY1" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405241i/789163.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Ashton could be considered an anti-hero in away. When we first meet Ashton, he’s this bad-boy party guy who is pretty laid back, yet when you get to know him more, there’s something about him that makes you just ache. He has a lot of past issues and it’s slowly uncovered throughout the read. And let me tell you, his secrets… wow. <br><br><b>My very honest emotions throughout </b><br><br><b>At 1%.... I was just like oh, I need to allocate 6 hours for his because I don’t want to put it down<br><br>At 27%... I was like OH.MY.GAH. NO!!!!! BUT secretly oh yes<br><br>At 42% … I am just swooning over Ash<br><br>At 70%... I am grabbing on to my tablet for dear life, b/c the tension is just killing me!<br><br>At 86%... I am about to explode<br><br>At 100%... I just felt like I had the best orgasm of my life! No joke girls. The ending… EPIC</b><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/mRZxgIJ" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405241i/789164.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I think what makes <i>One Tiny Lie</i> such a powerful and wonderful read to me is it’s so relatable. We all face hardships and we all have our coping mechanism, but sometimes, it just good to let go. You know? I adore this read, I truly do. <br><br><b>I love the story, I love the cover, I love the characters and I love you KA Tucker</b><br><br>KA Tucker has made it to my favorite authors list. I am so excited and happy for her visit to Houston, Texas. I just can’t wait!!!! <br><br>5 HUGE STARS!!!!<br><br><i>ARC provided by Atria Books via Netgalley in exchange for an honest review</i><br><br>For more reviews click - &gt; <a href="http://www.jacquelinesreads.blogspot.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Jacqueline's Reads</a></span>

<div id="review_558323132" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/558323132" />
    <a title="destini mia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13742215-destini-mia"><img alt="destini mia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1499903277p2/13742215.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/558323132?book_show_action=true">Mar 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="destini mia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="destini mia" href="/user/show/13742215-destini-mia">destini mia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer558323132" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5209226089020187299"><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1407775164ra/10763661.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>.<img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1407775164ra/10763662.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>*chuckles to self* that gif gets me every time . . . <br/><br/>Anyways, I <i>really</i> wanted to like this one. <i>
  <b>Really.</b>
</i> And to some extent I did, but it wasn't everything I thought it was going to be. <br/><br/><b>REACTION BEFORE READING</b><br/><blockquote>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1407775513ra/10763796.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</blockquote><br/><b>REACTION UPON FINISHING</b><br/><blockquote>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384265700ra/6830284.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</blockquote><br/><br/>So the basics before I commence ranting . . . <br/><br/>To some degree I liked the book. At some points, I was so interested and captivated with the story that I couldn't even think about putting it down . . . and then there were other times were I felt kind of bore</span>
  <span id="freeText5209226089020187299" style="display:none"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1407775164ra/10763661.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">.<img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1407775164ra/10763662.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>*chuckles to self* that gif gets me every time . . . <br><br>Anyways, I <i>really</i> wanted to like this one. <i>
  <b>Really.</b>
</i> And to some extent I did, but it wasn't everything I thought it was going to be. <br><br><b>REACTION BEFORE READING</b><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1407775513ra/10763796.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><b>REACTION UPON FINISHING</b><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384265700ra/6830284.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><br>So the basics before I commence ranting . . . <br><br>To some degree I liked the book. At some points, I was so interested and captivated with the story that I couldn't even think about putting it down . . . and then there were other times were I felt kind of bored and I started lightly skimming. When I put the book down, I didn't have that all-consuming urge to pick it back up again :( <br><br>I didn't feel a connection with the characters, especially Livie. She was just . . . <i>there</i> for me. Really innocent and really uptight. She just needed to relax, take a chill pill and: <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407778315i/10764285.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I enjoyed reading about the characters. but I didn't feel <i>in</i> the story. I read about some heartbreaking things that have happened to them, and don't get me wrong, I felt bad. You never want to hear about that happening to a person. But at the same time, I didn't take their pain as my own, you know? I just didn't <i>feel</i> it. <br><br><b>
  <u>On to the rant . . . spoilers ahead (they will be tagged). </u>
</b><br><br>I definitely should have done my research on this book because holy hell was I blindsided. <br><br> <b>Ashton.</b> First impression: he's a dick. Who thinks with his dick. And after a while I was ready to:<br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1407776470ra/10764059.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br>Then, a train wreck caring his <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[habit for cheating <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> comes my way. I don't like it . . . well, I pretty much hate it. But I can sometimes, maybe, look past it . . . ? Or at least make an attempt to understand. I get that sometimes, <b>shit happens.</b> It sucks, but it does. But here's when I really went WTF? <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ <i> <br><br>"It doesn't matter, Ashton. I just thought you regretted messing around on your girlfriend."<br><br>"I never said</i> that" <i>(...) "I just regretted messing around with</i> you."<br><br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1407776954ra/10764130.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br>Really, Ashton? Do you feel the <i>judging</i> coming from me? <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I get that you were forced into this, but come on? You made the girl fall in love with, have a little respect for her feelings. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><br>Another quote by Ashton that gave me the warm and fuzzies &lt;-- heavily laced with sarcasm.<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ <br><br><i>"Are you jealous, Irish?"<br><br>"Of what? That you're such a douche bag that you drop off your girlfriend and have another women in your bed within hours?"<br><br>"I didn't have anyone in my bed."<br><br>"You didn't?" I sigh with relief.<br><br>"He sakes his head, clicking his pen a few more times. "Up against the wall . . . in the shower . . ."</i><br><br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1407782309ra/10764804.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now you'd think I'd like Livie because of how she called him out on his shit. Well, she <i>says</i> one thing, but her <i>actions</i> say something else. I was kinda disappointed. <br><br>But in true Destini fashion, I ended up feeling a little bad for the guy. When I heard his full story, my heart went out to him. It doesn't change what he did, because he <b>definitely</b> could've handled thing with more finesse, but now I don't see him as <i>just</i> an asshole. Now I see him as an emotionally <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ and physically <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> scarred asshole. <br><br>On top of that, <i>One Tiny Lie</i> also had <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ a love triangle/square. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> My top two most hated things in one book.<br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1407782443ra/10764815.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><br>In the end, <br>My heart said 3.5 stars<br>&amp; my head said 2.5 stars<br>So 3 stars it is.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
