              <span id="reviewTextContainer484656662" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2877214214517881635"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401915i/780659._SY540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401915i/780660.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I need to preface my <s>rant</s> review with this: I loved, truly loved, Ten Tiny Breaths. I genuinely enjoy this author's writing. So it pains me to give this anything other than less than 4 or 5 stars, but I simply can't give it more than 3. This books was sadly a big let down for me, but only due to the plot. The writing was still fantastic. Unfortunately, there were issues in the plot that hit every single one of my no-no buttons. Minor spoilers below, and I'll block the major spoilers. You've been</span>
  <span id="freeText2877214214517881635" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401915i/780659._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401915i/780660.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I need to preface my <s>rant</s> review with this: I loved, truly loved, Ten Tiny Breaths. I genuinely enjoy this author's writing. So it pains me to give this anything other than less than 4 or 5 stars, but I simply can't give it more than 3. This books was sadly a big let down for me, but only due to the plot. The writing was still fantastic. Unfortunately, there were issues in the plot that hit every single one of my no-no buttons. Minor spoilers below, and I'll block the major spoilers. You've been warned.<br><br>When I first met Livie in One Tiny Lie, I really liked her. I couldn't wait to read the book where she was the heroine. As I began reading this, I began to get cold-sweat flashbacks to Keira from Thoughtless. (I was one of the few people that did NOT enjoy that book). <br><br>This was me for the majority of this book<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400567ra/776511.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I did not expect for this book to have a bit of a love triangle. Love triangles, yeaaaa.....<img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401915ra/780661.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But I digress. When Ashton is first introduced, I was all over that!<br><blockquote>
  <b>"He's pretty much the hottest guy at the school." She takes a sip of her beer. "And also a giant ass."<br>"That much I gathered."<br>"And a bit of a man whore."</b>
</blockquote><br><br>Those are the magic words for me, and a recipe for a great hero, but sadly it just didn't last.<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I take a huge issue with repetitive cheating. I can't handle it! It drives me nuts. And this book had it on both ends, from Ashton AND Livie. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>There was a whole lot of angst, which I normally don't mind. The constant push-pull, back and forth dance between Ashton and Livie drove me bat sh!t crazy. It was a whole bunch of<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401915ra/780662.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>followed by <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401915ra/780663.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Over and over and over and over...well you get the point<br><br>Livie was a big let down for me as well. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[She dates Connor because he's "right" for her, but she has the hots for Ashton. So the whole book she pretty much strings Connor along. Her reasoning? She doesn't want to hurt him. Seriously? Because fooling around with someone else and him later figuring it out isn't going to do that? Her inner monologue during all this?<br><blockquote>
<i>You can do this. Just keep being nice to him.</i> Just a few more days until I rip his heart out and stomp on it.</blockquote> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><br>I get that they're in college and Livie is only 18. But like I said, this is a huge hot button for me. I hate it. So it just killed the whole vibe of the book for me.<br><br>The 85% mark of this book was the straw that broke the camel's back for me. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Livie gives Ashton her virginity while her somewhat boyfriend, Connor, is downstairs at the party. The kicker? She knows Ashton has a girlfriend. The icing on the cake? What she doesn't know yet is that Ashton is engaged to said girlfriend now. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Yes there are reasons behind all this that we find out in the very last chapter of the book. For me, I already had such a solidified dislike for both of these characters, that it was a case of too little too late.<br><br>I can go on and on, but I need to cut myself off, or this will be the review that never ends.<br><br>Majority of the book is filled with this angst. We do get a HEA, but I thought the ending was very glossed over and rushed. <br><br>Don't get me wrong, there were still parts of the book that I enjoyed. I loved getting to catch up with Kacey and Trent. The interactions between Livie and her sister were hilarious. I also really liked the banter between Livie and Dr. Stayner. I loved his character. We also get more glimpses at the old gang, Ben, Storm, Dan and *swooning* Cain. Livie roommate, Reagan was also a riot to read. <br><br><br>Sadly that just wasn't enough to bring this book up to anything above 3 stars for me.<br><br>I just didn't find the title, One Tiny Lie, to be appropriate to what I read (there was nothing tiny about it). <br><br><b>For more reviews visit<br><a href="http://dirtygirlromance.com" target="blogspot" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436477285i/15465455._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_637774878" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/637774878" />
    <a title="Beatrice Masaluñga" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4590441-beatrice-masalu-ga"><img alt="Beatrice Masaluñga" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1603719912p2/4590441.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/637774878?book_show_action=true">Jul 22, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beatrice Masaluñga" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beatrice Masaluñga" href="/user/show/4590441-beatrice-masalu-ga">Beatrice Masaluñga</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4590441-beatrice-masalu-ga?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer637774878" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer99323679399815017">The second book in the <i>Ten Tiny Breaths</i> series features Kacey's younger sister, <b>Livie Cleary</b>. She handled the loss of their parents better than Kacey. She's resilient, coolheaded, mature and organized. Getting a glimpse of reality at the age of eleven, she took the responsibility of keeping themselves together when Kacey can't. If not for her love, care and patience, Kacey will further spiral into self-destruction. <br/><br/>Attending Princeton to pursue medicine is one of her lifelong dreams. She's going</span>
  <span id="freeText99323679399815017" style="display:none">The second book in the <i>Ten Tiny Breaths</i> series features Kacey's younger sister, <b>Livie Cleary</b>. She handled the loss of their parents better than Kacey. She's resilient, coolheaded, mature and organized. Getting a glimpse of reality at the age of eleven, she took the responsibility of keeping themselves together when Kacey can't. If not for her love, care and patience, Kacey will further spiral into self-destruction. <br /><br />Attending Princeton to pursue medicine is one of her lifelong dreams. She's going to dedicate herself to studies and stay out of trouble. Kacey say otherwise: Relax, have fun and live a little. One night, they get drunk on a party before the classes starts. Livie loosened up a little and had an intense drunk make-out session with the Princeton's Rowing team captain, <b>Ashton Henley</b>. He's a hot, egotistical womanizer who undeniably makes her heart beat faster. Later on, she meets his best friend and roommate Connor who happens to be her ideal guy. <br /><br /><i>What if her attraction to her ideal guy isn't as strong as she expected? <br />What if she wants Ashton more than ever but keeps pushing her away?<br /> What if her dreams was actually not the one she really wanted?</i><br /><br />There comes a point in life you feel lost and question everything. Your wants, goals, and expectations. I like Livie and Ash's story because they faced downfalls and rose up in the end. It's okay to make mistakes as long as you've learned from it and it's definitely okay to follow what you want than what others want you to be. It gives you freedom and happiness. As for the romance, I think their chemistry is good and not over the top. I just wish there's more flare to them. <br /><br /><b>Here are things I've encountered that gave me mixed feelings: </b><br />- I don't like Ashton constantly gives mixed signals to Livie. Both are mutually attracted with each other. I can't stand Ashton hurting and confusing her feelings. Like, c'mon man. <br />- Dr. Stayner's overfamiliarity. I don't know if it's just me. I understand he's like a guardian to the Cleary sisters but he shouldn't overstepped a line. Plus, his advices… nah. There are many things to have fun than going to a party. Also, what kind of shrink knocks on a dorm room early in the morning?! <br />- Kacey should tone down her wild side. Jesus C. Chill down woman!<br />- Most of the time, Livie overreacts on many things. It gets on my nerves.<br /><br />I think the highlight in this book is Ash's backstory. That one is heartbreaking. Overall, I like it despite of my issues on it. </span>
  <a data-text-id="99323679399815017" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1418884248" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1418884248" />
    <a title="Michelle " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/23450274-michelle"><img alt="Michelle " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1544751386p2/23450274.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1418884248?book_show_action=true">Oct 17, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michelle " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michelle " href="/user/show/23450274-michelle">Michelle </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23450274-michelle?shelf=made-me-cry">made-me-cry</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23450274-michelle?shelf=cracked-me-up">cracked-me-up</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23450274-michelle?shelf=college">college</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer1418884248&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1418884248" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12244121514696514299">3.5 and 4.5 Stars!<br/>So I HATE a love triangle book! Hate it I tell you! I also hate it even more when the girl KNOWS that she only has feelings for one of the guys but still holds onto the other. I also hate cheating! I will say that the only thing that kept me going was that she wasn't screwing them both. <br/>So this book just fucked me up! I had a love/hate relationship with it. I found myself growling through the entire book. lol<br/><br/>The book starts off with Livie moving into a dorm at Princeton. Kacey </span>
  <span id="freeText12244121514696514299" style="display:none">3.5 and 4.5 Stars!<br />So I HATE a love triangle book! Hate it I tell you! I also hate it even more when the girl KNOWS that she only has feelings for one of the guys but still holds onto the other. I also hate cheating! I will say that the only thing that kept me going was that she wasn't screwing them both. <br />So this book just fucked me up! I had a love/hate relationship with it. I found myself growling through the entire book. lol<br /><br />The book starts off with Livie moving into a dorm at Princeton. Kacey is there and dragging her to a toga party. Livie is to go to this party and she is under strict orders from the good Dr Stayner to let loose and have some fun. Kacey is there to make sure it happens. The drink of the night just happens to be Jell-O shots. After Livie has several and feeling the affects she's just sucked one in her mouth when the sexy beast Ashton slips his tongue in her mouth and steals it and also steams Livie up with a kiss that rocks her world. After Livie recovers she punches Ashton in the face. She's pissed that he just stole her first kiss. After Kacey blurts out that Livie is a virgin of everything Ashton and Livie do a lot of firsts. When she wakes up her head is a mess trying to remember everything that happened. <br />Livie gets dragged to another party with her roommate and there she sees Ashton with a beautiful girl who is his girlfriend. She is not happy that she was kissing on a guy that has a girlfriend. She hates Ashton's cheating ass! She then catches the eyes of Ashton's best friend Connor. Connor is the complete opposite of Ashton. He's sweet, smart and wants to take things slow with Livie. He's the perfect guy that her parents would of approved of her dating. He's not a cheating manwhore like Ashton. <br />So throughout most of the book (85%) Livie is dating sweet Connor but lusting over Ashton. Ashton also has a girlfriend that only visits on breaks. <br />Now Connor didn't give me goosebumps ever. He was nice and sweet but I didn't feel anything when him and Livie were together. But Ashton. Oh my! He gave me goosebumps! This tatted up muscle bulging sexy man was yummy! He was closed up tight. He didn't talk about his past but yet you just knew it wasn't filled with rainbows. I was dying for him to open up. <br />When Livie started to get him to open up my heart was breaking for him. Ashton is what made me love this book! Even though I couldn't figure out why the hell he kept telling Livie to stay with Connor. I knew Connor was going to end up getting his heart broke. They were suppose to be best friends. <br />Livie was the one I had a problem with. I needed her to tell Connor that they couldn't be together. Even if Ashton told her to stay with him. I needed her to man up and cut Connor loose. She grated my nerve with the thoughts she had about telling Connor and if he would break up with her. Then when it all came to a head how she acted toward him. I was growling I tell you! <br /><br />So anyway I'm done ranting about that. lol I will tell you that this one had more smexy in it than TTB. I did say smexy not smutty. Haha! <br /><br />I loved Ashton and Livie together. I loved that he called her Irish. I loved that we got more of the crazy Dr Stayner. I loved that we got more of Kacey and the rest of the gang. I also loved Livies roommate Reagan. <br /><br />I did NOT love that throughout almost all of the book Ashton had a girlfriend and Livie had a boyfriend. <br />That's why my rating is like it is. <br />Thank you for never giving me any details of Ashton and his girlfriend. I probably would of moved on to the next book if I had gotten even a hint that he was sleeping with her. <br />I'm off to read the next book. Yes! Because I'm loving this series! <br /><br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_483701154" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/483701154" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/483701154?book_show_action=true">Dec 23, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=emotional-angsty-books">emotional-angsty-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer483701154" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3091578106082393514">While <i>Ten Tiny Breaths</i> was about one person obviously spinning out of control, this book is the opposite. Livie is very much in control or so it seems. Kacey is always looking out for her sister and this time, she's enlisted the help of Dr. Stayner to help Livie actually <i>live</i>. <br/><br/><b>WOW</b>...this book had all the elements I love but most especially, it had all the emotional drama. I could not put it down and literally read it in one day. I'm not really sure why I loved it so much more than <i>Ten Tiny Breat</i></span>
  <span id="freeText3091578106082393514" style="display:none">While <i>Ten Tiny Breaths</i> was about one person obviously spinning out of control, this book is the opposite. Livie is very much in control or so it seems. Kacey is always looking out for her sister and this time, she's enlisted the help of Dr. Stayner to help Livie actually <i>live</i>. <br><br><b>WOW</b>...this book had all the elements I love but most especially, it had all the emotional drama. I could not put it down and literally read it in one day. I'm not really sure why I loved it so much more than <i>Ten Tiny Breaths</i> because they are similar. I guess I just loved seeing Livie come out of her shell. <br><br>When I heard Livie was getting her own book, I wasn't really excited. I mean, she was a sweet girl in Kacey's book and I just couldn't imagine what KAT could do that could make me enjoy the book. I'm sooo happy I decided to read it. <br><br>Livie is three years older and off to Princeton to go to college. As I mentioned before, Kacey got Dr. Stayner's help in bringing Livie out of her shell so all summer they have been doing crazy things and that doesn't end with Livie going to Princeton. Kacey is there to see her off in style and almost one of the first things is getting her drunk at a toga party. <br><br>Enter Ashton...aka Jello thief, aka rowing captain, aka has a girlfriend, aka man whore, aka majorly broken, aka wants "Irish". Ashton is everything Livie's heart wants but <i>nothing</i> her brain says she should have so she fights it all the way. Ashton doesn't let her get away easily...even thought he really tries to push her away! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379793741i/582140.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I loved Livie and Ashton together. Something about them just worked. Yes...they have A LOT of roadblocks and they both don't do the right thing. I guess that's it...the pull they have on each other and that they just can't stay away. Ashton gives Livie quite the education...I wish things were a bit more detailed though! And he was sooo romantic! I loved the five reasons and the picture and of course, how he always called Livie "Irish". ~sigh~ <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379793741i/582139.jpg" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I loved all the characters in the book. Livie's dorm mate, Rachel, was hilarious and Ashton's roommates were great too. Dr. Stayner really shined in this book and I have a feeling that will continue. But mostly, I loved the relationship between Kacey and Livie and of course, reading more about Kacey and Trent! ♥ <br><br>We do get lots of drama and a lot of people won't like it. If you really want to know....<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[there's cheating. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I'm always torn about that but it was a big part of how Ashton dealt with being so broken...and that's quite a story! :( <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379793741i/582138.jpg" width="300" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There are a lot of other sad issues in this book...child abuse, death, cancer and Alzheimer's. The twins were really sweet though and I loved what they brought to the story. <br><br>Probably the only thing that bothered me was the ending. Just like the epilogue in <i>Ten Tiny Breaths</i>, I felt things tied up too perfectly! <br><br>The next book is <i>Four Seconds To Lose</i> and it's supposed to be Cain's book. Again, I'm not sure how I feel about that since we don't know Cain very well <b>but</b>...after this book, I'm going to trust KAT to do her magic! I heard there will be a fourth book and it will be Ben's....now, that's one I will be looking forward to!<br><br><br>Favorite quotes:<br><br>♦ Ashton “I Regret You” Henley.<br><br>♥ "Irish loves Ashton"<br><br>♥ “Because you’re not a one-night girl, Irish.” Leaning in to place a kiss on my jawline, he whispers, “You’re my forever girl.”<br><br>♥ 1. I’m brilliant <br>2. I’m charming <br>3. I’m hung like a thoroughbred <br>4. I’ve stopped all philandering <br>5. I’m highly skilled, as you’ve learned the other night. <br><br>P.S. Stop staring at my hands. I know what you want me to with them.<br><br>♥ "It was . . . incredible. It feels <i>right</i> in a way that nothing else has ever felt right."<br><br>♦ “He’s five hundred for two hours!” Swinging her hand Ashton’s way, she adds, “Seven-fifty for him because he’s young. You should hear how he makes my sister scream!”</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="3091578106082393514" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_632144980" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/632144980" />
    <a title="Ash Wednesday" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10484016-ash-wednesday"><img alt="Ash Wednesday" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1379043440p2/10484016.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/632144980?book_show_action=true">Jun 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ash Wednesday" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ash Wednesday" href="/user/show/10484016-ash-wednesday">Ash Wednesday</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">fans of Avoiding Commitment and Irish Things </span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=college">college</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=review">review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=netgalley">netgalley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=arc">arc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer632144980" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9235799660467534222"><b>
  <i>3.5 STARS<br/><br/>"Go forth, and make thy mistakes."</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424023i/845151.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>So I gave <i>Ten Tiny Breaths</i> pretty much the same rating but I might just like this a smidge better. So much so that the latent soap opera watcher in me may have enjoyed this a little too inappropriately that I've been sorely tempted to give it an outright 4. But where this book fell short, it fell a little too hard. So much so that I can't really find it in myself to rave and recommend it to anyone without expecting some backlash.<br/><br/>Livie Clearey's live</span>
  <span id="freeText9235799660467534222" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>3.5 STARS<br><br>"Go forth, and make thy mistakes."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424023i/845151.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So I gave <i>Ten Tiny Breaths</i> pretty much the same rating but I might just like this a smidge better. So much so that the latent soap opera watcher in me may have enjoyed this a little too inappropriately that I've been sorely tempted to give it an outright 4. But where this book fell short, it fell a little too hard. So much so that I can't really find it in myself to rave and recommend it to anyone without expecting some backlash.<br><br>Livie Clearey's lived her life following the path and structure her parents seem to have designed for her. Straight A's in high school. Pre-med at Princeton. Med-school to get into Pediatric Oncology (which, sidenote, is all sorts of warning signs because nobody in pre-med and and very few in medschool wants to get on that depressing train). That was until her sister Kacey and her therapist intervenes who through a series of (ridiculous) non-therapy sessions eventually lands her smack in the middle of the bermuda triangle of her, Ashton (the wrong kind of right guy) and Connor (the right kind of wrong guy).<br><br>You really want to recommend THAT trope to anyone without some Xanax handy?<br><br><u>
  <b>The Good</b>
</u><br><br>✔ One of the reasons why I jumped this ARC is because while I wasn't the biggest fan of TTB's plot twist towards the end, KA Tucker's writing fits this genre very well. Very easy on the eyes and the brains, no unnecessary whoring of adjectives or excessive scene exposition. <b>The storytelling feels clean, the dialogue sharp (most of the time) and the characters consistent (again, most of the time) which always does great service to mostly predictable plot lines.</b><br><br>✔ I appreciate that <b>the drama on this one was <u>relatively</u> restrained compared to TTB. </b>The plot twist didn't give me too much of a whiplash that the story begins to blur the lines of realistic fiction and fantasy. Most of the story points were believable as much as I guess the drama in <i>Gossip Girl</i> was believable (specifically season 1 and 2, I KNOW that's not saying much).<br><br>✔ I actually liked Livie... outside of the love triangle. Her burden of walking a path made for her and not of her own choosing was very relatable to me.<b> I liked the contrast of how Ashton seems like a carefree character but yearns for freedom while Livie shies away from it because she doesn't know what to do with hers. </b><br><br><u>
  <b>The Bad </b>
</u><br><br>✘ <b>At the heart of this book was a very, poorly designed love triangle which only sets out to make the participants act like dickholes and asshats.</b> I'm very forgiving towards manwhores and quite lax with cheating in books if the cause can convince me. But Livie didn't merit enough emotional conflict to string along two guys at the same time. She's a smart girl and the choice was made so very obvious yet she hung on to the other guy while lusting after the other making her come off as a selfish horndog.<br><br>And no, owning up to it in the end doesn't make it okay.<br><br>✘ Ashton is a puzzle to me. I do love his backstory and his Livie-related antics were mostly cute. What I don't get is how he had those past experiences and still have the predilection to "man-handle" Livie especially in the early chapters. I wish the effects <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[of his father's abuse <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> were given some detail and depth instead of just focusing on the abuse itself. <br><br>✘ <b>All of the Kacey-Trent appearances still made me squirm</b> because of their own blend of cray. I'm still not sold on their HEA.<br><br>✘ I was not a fan of using the Deus ex Machina resolution.. well, of everything. <b>Using one character as the device to resolve every single issue raised in the story was pushing it a little too far.</b> It leads to question why <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Ashton <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> didn't do ALL those things before and thus avoiding the unsavory aftertaste of the character acting out on his drama. <br><br>✘ And speaking of drama:<b> the cancer kids subplot could've been handled better. </b>It felt trying a little too hard in making me feel something. They're kids. With cancer. You really don't want to pile on the tearjerkers beyond that because you'd just end up making me feel like I'm getting manipulated to cry.<br><br><br><u>
  <b>The <s>Ugly</s>Irish</b>
</u><br><br><b>To much Irish-ing!</b> It reminds me of what little I read of <i>Beautiful Disaster</i> with all the Pigeon-ing. I really wish someone would do something about this for the actual published edition because it was REALLY annoying.There was a stretch of conversation between Ashton and Livie where his every turn of phrase ended with "Irish" which I can't quote because of the publishers' restrictions but this might do:<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Ash: here are your fries, Irish.<br>Liv: Thanks Ash, can you pass me the salt please?<br>Ash: Those fries are salty enough, Irish. You can't risk gaining your first fifteen seeing as you can't jog without tripping, Irish.<br>Liv: but it's organic potatoes!<br>Ash: nope sorry, Irish. Gonna go out in the rain and run shirtless now, Irish. The world implores me to.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Get it? Irish? Potatoes? Ah, fuck it. <br><br>I'm gonna wrap up this up because I may have gotten carried away (again). Overall, I did enjoy this book just not something I'm brave enough to recommend to anyone. But I'd still grab the last book in this series hoping KA Tucker's great writing will find the perfect plausible story to match it and finally hook me in.<br><br><i>ARC provided by Atria Books via Netgalley in exchange for an unbiased, honest review.</i></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="9235799660467534222" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_476107333" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/476107333" />
    <a title=" Megan • Reading Books Like a Boss (book blog)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2607684-megan-reading-books-like-a-boss-book-blog"><img alt=" Megan • Reading Books Like a Boss (book blog)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1486609762p2/2607684.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/476107333?book_show_action=true">Dec 12, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title=" Megan • Reading Books Like a Boss (book blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name=" Megan • Reading Books Like a Boss (book blog)" href="/user/show/2607684-megan-reading-books-like-a-boss-book-blog"> Megan • Reading Books Like a Boss (book blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2607684-megan-reading-books-like-a-boss-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2607684-megan-reading-books-like-a-boss-book-blog?shelf=audiobooked-it">audiobooked-it</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer476107333" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2139467673205177231"><a href='http://readingbookslikeaboss.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400647i/776761._SX540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>Check out my other reviews at<a href='http://readingbookslikeaboss.com' rel='nofollow noopener'> Reading Books Like a Boss</a></b><br/><br/>My Rating: <a href='http://readingbookslikeaboss.com/tag/4-5-stars/' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400647i/776762.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><i>I received a copy via NetGalley in exchange for an honest review.</i><br/><br/>After the tragic death of their parents, Kacey and Livie were forced to grow up fast. In Ten Tiny Breaths, we saw Kacey struggle with the trauma of losing her parents. For years, Kacey bottled up her emotions and behaved badly, and it all came crashing down. Through Kacey’s point-of-view, it appears Livie dealt with her parents’ death extremely well, much bet</span>
  <span id="freeText2139467673205177231" style="display:none"><a href="http://readingbookslikeaboss.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400647i/776761._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Check out my other reviews at<a href="http://readingbookslikeaboss.com" rel="nofollow noopener"> Reading Books Like a Boss</a></b><br><br>My Rating: <a href="http://readingbookslikeaboss.com/tag/4-5-stars/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400647i/776762.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>I received a copy via NetGalley in exchange for an honest review.</i><br><br>After the tragic death of their parents, Kacey and Livie were forced to grow up fast. In Ten Tiny Breaths, we saw Kacey struggle with the trauma of losing her parents. For years, Kacey bottled up her emotions and behaved badly, and it all came crashing down. Through Kacey’s point-of-view, it appears Livie dealt with her parents’ death extremely well, much better than her sister.<br><br>However, everything is not as it seems.<br><br>One Tiny Lie takes place a few years after Ten Tiny Breaths. Livie is on her way to Princeton for college, fulfilling her father’s dream of attending his alma mater. She has maintained a spotless academic record and has never gone through any teenage rebellions. Concerned that Livie hasn’t really dealt with their parents’ deaths, Kacey recommends that she chat with Dr. Stayner, Kacey’s therapist.<br><br>Dr. Stayner is not your typical “lay-down-on-the-white-couch-and-let’s-talk” therapist. His tactics and methodologies are anything but conventional. In fact, they border on crazy. The summer before college, he subjects Livie to a summer full of dares and tasks to complete, and she excels at all of them. For as long as she can remember, Livie has wanted to be a pediatric oncologist, but these weekly chats with Dr. Stayner make Livie question what she really wants for her future. Her whole life has been building to this one goal of becoming a doctor, but is this what she really wants?<br><br>Kacey takes Livie to her first college party to initiate her into college life. What Livie doesn’t know until later is that this is part of Dr. Stayner’s therapy plan. Essentially, Dr. Stayner gives Livie a prescription for tequila and debauchery. Craziness ensues in the form of stolen Jell-O shots. Livie meets Ashton, the hot-shot captain of the Princeton rowing team and said Jell-O shot thief. After a night of drunken make-out sessions, Livie and Ashton are drawn to each other. The problem is that Ashton is not available and has a sort of playboy reputation on campus. Livie eventually moves on with Connor in hopes of forgetting about Ashton.<br><br>What I loved about Ashton and Livie was their chemistry. There are very few book couples that give me this feeling. I couldn’t get enough of them and I just wanted them to just BE TOGETHER. Every time they were together there were sparks and feel-good fizzies. I just wanted to scream, “Just do it already!” When a scene with them ended, I couldn’t wait until I had more Livie and Ashton time. The romance between the two of them had them forbidden aspect that I loved. Ashton was in a daddy-arranged relationship with a girl, but he wasn’t in love with her. And Livie was in a relationship with Connor, the safe guy. There was a (sort-of) love-triangle in it, so if that sort of thing bothers you you should probably stay clear of it.<br><br>Aside from the romantic aspect of their relationship, I loved seeing them work out their problems with each other and with themselves. As Livie struggles to find her identity in something other than being a doctor, Ashton is there to sweetly support her. The things Ashton does for Livie are extremely selfless and show exactly how he feels about her.<br><br>Ashton and Livie are one of the most passionate and unforgettable couples in a book that I have read this year. I will rereading One Tiny Lie again and again and again. <br><br>Favorite Quotes:<br><blockquote>
<br>“The only thing I regret is that it ever ended. And I’m the one who’s jealous. Insanely so.”<br><br>“1.) I’m brilliant<br>2.) I’m charming<br>3.) I’m hung like a thoroughbred<br>4.) I’ve stopped all philandering<br>5.) I’m highly skilled, as you’ve learned the other night.<br>P.S. Stop staring at my hands. I know what you want me to do with them.”<br><br>“I feel as though I’ve entered some strange twilight zone where everything I know has been turned upside down.”</blockquote><br><br>_________________________<br><br><strong>Find more of my reviews and other bookish things here:</strong><br><br><strong>✥ My blog <a href="http://readingbookslikeaboss.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">R</a><a href="http://readingbookslikeaboss.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">eading Books Like a Boss</a></strong><br><strong> ✥ Like on <a href="https://www.facebook.com/ReadingBooksLikeABoss" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a></strong><br><strong> ✥ Follow on <a href="http://twitter.com/ireadlikeaboss" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a></strong></span>
  <a data-text-id="2139467673205177231" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_632947445" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/632947445" />
    <a title="Jen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6049062-jen"><img alt="Jen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460575899p2/6049062.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/632947445?book_show_action=true">Jun 04, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen" href="/user/show/6049062-jen">Jen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=kindle-own">kindle-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=new-adult-romance">new-adult-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=october-reads">october-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer632947445" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3156629342876338073">I battled with the rating on this one, mainly because the writing is very good. What made me rate this a 3.5 stars is the fact that I wasn't expecting the story to go in the direction it did for Livie's book. This story has a love triangle in it; and I am not a big fan of those kinds of story lines at all. If I am made aware of it before I start reading the book then I might prepare myself and read it anyway. In the case of "One Tiny Lie," I wasnt expecting it, and it just made me apprehensive t</span>
  <span id="freeText3156629342876338073" style="display:none">I battled with the rating on this one, mainly because the writing is very good. What made me rate this a 3.5 stars is the fact that I wasn't expecting the story to go in the direction it did for Livie's book. This story has a love triangle in it; and I am not a big fan of those kinds of story lines at all. If I am made aware of it before I start reading the book then I might prepare myself and read it anyway. In the case of "One Tiny Lie," I wasnt expecting it, and it just made me apprehensive through out the whole time I was reading. Unfortunately, it did take away from my reading experience, and if I am honest I did grumble about it the whole way through!<br /><br />The thing is though, the story wasn't all bad and there was some very beautiful parts to it. I would have liked to see more positive things going on though for Livie. In the first book that was about Livie's sister; Livie was just so bright and positive. In this one, there were a lot more negative scenes, and I can't help but look at the heroine in a love triangle and get resentful because they are not being honest with the guy she is holding on a string. So my respect for Livie dropped, and I kept having flashbacks about the book "Thoughless!!" (I will say Livie was not near as bad as that heroine!LOL)<br /><br />One of the main themes in the story was the choices we make and how it is important to make the choices that are going to make us happy in our lives, as opposed to living your life for everyone else and being unhappy while doing it. One of my favorite quotes by K.A. Tucker is this:<br /><br />"Life has a funny way of creating its own tests. It thrws curve balls that make you do and think and feel things that are in direct conflict with what you had planned and don't allow you to operate in terms of black and white."<br /><br />The truth of the matter is that I could relate to Livie and her impulsive desire to please others at her own expense. When she was so busy worrying about what others would think, and making them happy; she lost sight of who she really was inside, and what she truly wanted in her life to make her happy. It is a hard way to live, and finally the pressure became too much for her. That is when the quirky Dr. Stayner comes in to the picture to and gives her a hand. I love this shrink! He was in the first book, and helped Livie's sister in a big unconventional way! He is hilarious, and rough around the edges; but he whips his pupils into tip top shape in no time!<br /><br />I don't want to go into details of the book as it is a love triangle and I wouldn't want to give anything away. On the whole, this was a good story, and I grew to love one of the guys; Ashton. He is way more than what he seems on his surface; yes, he is hot,tattooed and built; but there is so much more to him. He doesn't let people into his core self at all, and he holds a ton of secrets. When Livie and him start taking the journey into getting to know one another, there are a lot of surprises along the way that they find out about one another. It is entertaining; but it is not a smooth ride; because right around the corner is his best friend Connor, and Connor is the "perfect" guy that Livie "should" go for. Who will Livie choose in the end? Or maybe she will walk away empty handed? If you are the type of reader who loves a great triangle, then this is a must read for you. K.A. Tucker definitely has talent as a writer, and I am eager to read the third book coming out shortly that is about the strip club owner from the first book in the series. In my opinion, this is an author that is on the rise to success. She sure has talent!</span>
  <a data-text-id="3156629342876338073" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_614854119" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/614854119" />
    <a title="♥Rachel♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5481477-rachel"><img alt="♥Rachel♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1363996055p2/5481477.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/614854119?book_show_action=true">May 13, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♥Rachel♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♥Rachel♥" href="/user/show/5481477-rachel">♥Rachel♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer614854119" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15550087182605635470">I was surprised to find out how much I really loved <b>One Tiny Lie</b>. I had started reading it with a lot of apprehension because I found out there was cheating in the story, and I HATE cheating stories. It almost always ruins the story for me. Why did I start reading when I knew this? Well, first of all I requested this title before I knew about the cheating. Second, I was assured that the story was really good in spite of the hated subject. I have to agree with that. <br/><br/>Livie Cleary is the sister who</span>
  <span id="freeText15550087182605635470" style="display:none">I was surprised to find out how much I really loved <b>One Tiny Lie</b>. I had started reading it with a lot of apprehension because I found out there was cheating in the story, and I HATE cheating stories. It almost always ruins the story for me. Why did I start reading when I knew this? Well, first of all I requested this title before I knew about the cheating. Second, I was assured that the story was really good in spite of the hated subject. I have to agree with that. <br /><br />Livie Cleary is the sister who was very much overlooked in the previous book because her sister Kacey was such a train wreck. Kacey was in the accident that killed their parents and left her in rehab for a year, so Livie had to be strong because her sister was not. Now that most of Kacey’s demons have been dealt with, all eyes turn to Livie because no one can be that perfect and not crack at some point. Dr. Stayner, Kacey’s <i>very</i> unconventional therapist, basically forces his guidance on Livie. Not even letting up when Livie leaves Miami for Princeton. He keeps trying to get Livie to look at her life, make sure all the decisions she’s making is because she wants them and not because she is leading the life she thinks her parents would’ve expected her to. So with the advice to make some mistakes, and to loosen way-the-heck-up, Livie starts college.<br /><br />Enter Ashton. He’s beautiful, and Livie’s drunk at her first college party, and they can’t keep their hands or their mouths off each other! Livie finds out that Ashton has a girlfriend and resolves to stay away from him, writing him off as a man-whore jerk. Life has other plans when she strikes up a friendship with his best friend, Connor. Connor is everything her parents would approve of. He’s a steady guy, serious student, and comes from a solid family. He’s good looking as well, but there’s no spark. However, because Livie feels this is the type of guy she should be with, she doesn’t say no when he asks her to date. Being that Connor and Ashton live in the same house and are best friends their paths cross, often….<br /><br /> So yes, this sounds like a recipe for disaster if you hate cheating, right? Well, here is why I think it worked for me: I think the author did a wonderful job conveying Livie’s naiveté, as well as showing how very young she is for her age. She makes mistakes, stupid mistakes, but they are realistic “being young” mistakes, AND they are not done with malicious intent. Livie fully intends to stay away from Ashton, and Ashton away from Livie, BUT they end up together and their chemistry and connection make short work of their resolve. Have you ever been with someone that you just click with intensely, you’re drawn to them like a magnet? This is Ashton and Livie. Plus, the whole Connor relationship is one that just sort of happens to Livie, he just keeps making the next date, and she doesn’t say no. I know, messed up. Another reason I was able to stomach this is because there were hints that all wasn’t as it seemed with Ashton and his girlfriend, or his life. <br /><br />I’m not saying that I agree or even condone what happened, but I don’t always have to like the actions or behavior of characters to enjoy the story. If I can understand the motivations and reasons for their transgressions, I can look past them. I did with Livie and Ashton. They just clicked for me and I wanted everything to work out for them. They clearly cared so much for each other, they just needed to sort their <s>shit</s> baggage out! <br /><br />I have ten pages worth of highlights showing how much I loved this story. Here’s one of my favorites:<br /><br />When pressed to come up with some redeeming qualities, this is Ashton’s note to Livie while in English class:<b><br /><br />1. I’m brilliant<br />2. I’m charming<br />3. I’m hung like a thoroughbred<br />4. I’ve stopped all philandering<br />5. I’m highly skilled, as you’ve learned the other night<br /><br />P.S. Stop staring at my hands. I know what you want me to do with them. <br /></b><br /><br />One Tiny Lie was captivating story of two people finding the strength to live the life they want and chose to, instead of a life decided by guilt or expectation. I’m so happy I read One Tiny Lie in spite of my reservations, because I ended up really loving it. <br /><i><br />A copy was provided by Atria Books through Netgalley in exchange for an honest review. Thank you!<br /><br />*Quote taken from an uncorrected proof and may change in the final copy.</i><br /><br />You can read this review and more at <a href="http://thereadersden.blogspot.com/2013/09/review-one-tiny-lie-by-ka-tucker.html" rel="nofollow noopener">The Readers Den.</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="15550087182605635470" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_487783070" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/487783070" />
    <a title="Amy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11588440-amy"><img alt="Amy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1451259033p2/11588440.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/487783070?book_show_action=true">Dec 28, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Amy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amy" href="/user/show/11588440-amy">Amy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11588440-amy?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer487783070" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15376896210227980983">5 bright, shiny stars!! I love love loved it!!!!<br/><br/>One Tiny Lie is Livie’s story. You may remember her as Kacey’s younger sister in <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15990969.Ten_Tiny_Breaths__Ten_Tiny_Breaths___1_' title='Ten Tiny Breaths (Ten Tiny Breaths, #1) by K.A. Tucker' rel='nofollow noopener'>Ten Tiny Breaths</a>. If you haven’t read that yet, I highly recommend you do as it was one of my favorite books of 2012 :)<br/><br/><a href='http://photobucket.com/' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402375i/782047.jpg' alt=' photo livie.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Livie lost her parents 7 years ago in a tragic drunk driving accident. She was only 11 at the time, but she still clings to her dad’s last words to her. <br/><br/><b>
  <i>“That’s my Livie Girl. Make me proud.”</i>
</b><br/><br/>She’s currently living out her dreams at Princeton as</span>
  <span id="freeText15376896210227980983" style="display:none">5 bright, shiny stars!! I love love loved it!!!!<br><br>One Tiny Lie is Livie’s story. You may remember her as Kacey’s younger sister in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15990969.Ten_Tiny_Breaths__Ten_Tiny_Breaths___1_" title="Ten Tiny Breaths (Ten Tiny Breaths, #1) by K.A. Tucker" rel="nofollow noopener">Ten Tiny Breaths</a>. If you haven’t read that yet, I highly recommend you do as it was one of my favorite books of 2012 :)<br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402375i/782047.jpg" alt=" photo livie.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Livie lost her parents 7 years ago in a tragic drunk driving accident. She was only 11 at the time, but she still clings to her dad’s last words to her. <br><br><b>
  <i>“That’s my Livie Girl. Make me proud.”</i>
</b><br><br>She’s currently living out her dreams at Princeton as a pre-med major.<br> <br>On the advice of her sister, she’s been talking weekly to Kacey’s psychiatrist, Dr. Stayner. Can I just say, I loved Dr. Stayner. I think I need him in my life to help sort everything out. Seriously, he was a hoot!!<br><br>Dr. Stayner is helping Livie realize that her dreams may not be her dreams at all. Instead, they are a way for her to cling to the life her parents wanted her to have.<br><br><b>
  <i>“I think your parents helped create that plan and you are holding on to it for dear life as a way of holding on to them.”</i>
</b><br><br>Livie’s first night on campus she meets Ashton Henley, hottest guy at school... arrogant... sexy crooked smirk... dimples... a bit of a manwhore... tortured past. I was instantly hooked. And then he opened his mouth. (swoon)<br><br><b>
  <i>“Because you’re not a one-night girl, Irish.”<br><br>Leaning in to place a kiss on my jawline, he whispers, “You’re my forever girl.”</i>
</b><br><br>Oh. Em. Gee. I think I drooled on my Kindle. <br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402375i/782048.jpg" alt=" photo ashton.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>There are a lot of mixed signals from Ash. There is a lot of cheating since Ash has a girlfriend and Livie has started dating his best friend, Connor. There are a lot of secrets from Ash’s past. And a lot of revelations in Livie’s life as she discovers the future she had planned may not be what she wants at all.<br><br>I thoroughly enjoyed this book and look forward to more from K.A. Tucker!!<br><br><i>ARC received via NetGalley in exchange for an honest review.</i></span>

<div id="review_978236859" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/978236859" />
    <a title="Jasmine" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31339793-jasmine"><img alt="Jasmine" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406624675p2/31339793.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/978236859?book_show_action=true">Jun 26, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jasmine" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jasmine" href="/user/show/31339793-jasmine">Jasmine</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=standalones">standalones</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=all-time-fav-author">all-time-fav-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=i-love-me-some-angst-drama">i-love-me-some-angst-drama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=imma-hit-that-bitch">imma-hit-that-bitch</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=killing-me-with-sexual-tension">killing-me-with-sexual-tension</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=im-gonna-need-therapy">im-gonna-need-therapy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=motha-whiplash-emotions">motha-whiplash-emotions</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=love-triangles-be-damned">love-triangles-be-damned</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer978236859" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9612863892881886337"><b><s>4.5 STARS<br/>3 STARS</s><br/>4 EMOTIONAL WHIPLASH STARS! ★★★★ </b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408897897i/10909487.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>”How do you figure out the right way to live your life?”</i>
</b><br/><br/>First off, let me say that I absolutely loved <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15990969.Ten_Tiny_Breaths__Ten_Tiny_Breaths___1_' title='Ten Tiny Breaths (Ten Tiny Breaths, #1) by K.A. Tucker' rel='nofollow noopener'>Ten Tiny Breaths</a> and when I learnt that Livie was getting her own book, I was super excited. KA Tucker delivered some amazing, powerful writing in TTB and I thought this is sure right up my alley again.<br/><br/>But oh boy, <b>
  <i>I sure as hell didn’t expect</i>
</b> that this book would rekindle all that vicious feelings I had with SC Stephens’ <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13517535.Thoughtless__Thoughtless___1_' title='Thoughtless (Thoughtless, #1) by S.C. Stephens' rel='nofollow noopener'>Thoughtless</a>. I wan</span>
  <span id="freeText9612863892881886337" style="display:none"><b><s>4.5 STARS<br>3 STARS</s><br>4 EMOTIONAL WHIPLASH STARS! ★★★★ </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408897897i/10909487.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>”How do you figure out the right way to live your life?”</i>
</b><br><br>First off, let me say that I absolutely loved <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15990969.Ten_Tiny_Breaths__Ten_Tiny_Breaths___1_" title="Ten Tiny Breaths (Ten Tiny Breaths, #1) by K.A. Tucker" rel="nofollow noopener">Ten Tiny Breaths</a> and when I learnt that Livie was getting her own book, I was super excited. KA Tucker delivered some amazing, powerful writing in TTB and I thought this is sure right up my alley again.<br><br>But oh boy, <b>
  <i>I sure as hell didn’t expect</i>
</b> that this book would rekindle all that vicious feelings I had with SC Stephens’ <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13517535.Thoughtless__Thoughtless___1_" title="Thoughtless (Thoughtless, #1) by S.C. Stephens" rel="nofollow noopener">Thoughtless</a>. I wanted to douse my Kindle with gasoline &amp; set it on fire but on the other extreme, I wanted to say “Screw this shit, let me love you!”. <b>OH DEAR GOD HELP ME.</b><br><br>That being said, I’m gonna put it out there now that this book contains <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[cheating and love triangle/square <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> which technically sums up to two things that drive me absolutely fucking nuts when I read any book. <br><br>************<br><br><b>One Tiny Lie</b> is the story of <b>Livie Cleary</b>, the little sister of Kacey from TTB. In TTB, Livie has always been the calm and collective, non-impulsive sister. Now that she’s about to enter Princeton, will she be prepared to face a whole new world and leave the comforts of her newfound home in Miami? <br><br>Then comes one crazy night of Jell-O shots at a college party. With the help of Kacey (and also by their ever-loving psychiatrist, Dr Stayner’s orders LOL), our perfect, straight-As girl had her Jell-O shot AND her first kiss snatched by the Jell-O thief aka <b>Ashton Henley</b>. With even more shots later, let’s say the night was a complete cray-cray.<br><br>Next day, it was just mostly awkward encounters between Livie &amp; Ashton and the usual brush-off event AND THEN BAM! In comes <b>Mr “Connor from Dublin”</b> who sweeps Livie off her feet and oh, did I mention, <b>he is Ashton’s best friend AND housemate?</b> <br><br><b>DING DING DING. WARNING BELLS. DEJA VU THOUGHTLESS ALERT. </b><br><br>In summary, we have:<br><b>Livie</b>: Superbly attracted to Ashton but can’t be with him. Dates Connor because he’s the “perfect example” of a guy she needs in her life.<br><b>Ashton</b>: Superbly attracted to Livie but can’t be with her. Already has a girlfriend (Dana) and is Connor’s best friend &amp; housemate.<br><b>Connor</b>: Loves Livie and believes is the perfect girl for him; beautiful and smart. Truly cares about Ashton despite the manwhore that he is. <br><br><s>AND LET THE GAMES BEGIN.</s> And so it begins, that awful vicious cycle of events.<br><br>************<br><br><b>
  <u>What I loved:</u>
</b><br><br><b>The main theme of this book.</b> As usual, KA Tucker delivers that superbly well just like in TTB. It’s <b>emotional, powerful and raw</b> &amp; it will bring you to the brink of tears when you <b>feel</b> for these characters. This book is all about <b>making choices even when you don’t know what is the right or wrong one.</b> It’s about self-discovery, living a life that makes <b>
  <i>you</i>
</b> happy as opposed to living one for the sake of happiness of others.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> "Life has a funny way of creating its own tests. It throws curve balls that make you do and think and feel things that are in direct conflict with what you had planned and don't allow you to operate in terms of black and white." </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1399616009ra/9575348.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And in a true KA Tucker fashion story, we have a broken soul that is Ashton. You will feel a multitude of emotions for this guy; <b>you will hate him, you will love him, you will want to rip his balls off, you will want to hug &amp; cry with him.</b> But most of all, you will still want to root for him and Livie despite everything ♥<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> "I don't have all the pieces to fix this beautiful, trapped, broken man, but I do have one piece and it's mine to give. For one night, for all nights. For however long he wants it. Me. Completely.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401244ra/778524.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lastly, the winner of this entire book would be <b>Dr Stayner.</b> He’s the most awesome shrink on the planet, nuff’ said. I would have no doubt that he possesses Jedi mind tricks which makes him wickedly awesome.<br><br><b>
  <u>What ticked me off:</u>
</b><br><br>It would be fairly obvious to say that <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[the repetitive cheating <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> totally set me off. What makes it way worse would be <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[repetitive from BOTH Livie and Ashton <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. I have some SERIOUS problem trying to grasp why <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Livie kept on stringing Connor in when she obviously knows where her heart lies. I’m a firm believer of brutal honesty when it comes to a relationship &amp; the fact that she even thinks that breaking it off later would lessen the blow, NOT TRUE. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400515546ra/9684396.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And then you know that 85% scene, <b>HOLY RAGE OF EMOTIONS. </b><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Can’t believe they were happily canoodling on the bed when Connor was right downstairs (holy shit, brings back so much anger I had with Kiera in Thoughtless). And then the complete WTF moment when Dana comes in and DROPS THAT NEWS BOMB. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408897897ra/10909488.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>************<br><br>So after calming myself down, I thought hard and through on how to rate this one...and I decided that it wouldn’t be completely fair to slash the rating so badly due to how the entire thing played out. This is after all an <b>angst-driven book &amp; they’re 18 and mostly naive and shit happens all the time.</b> <br><br>And so, <b>4 stars it is.</b> Mainly because <b>KA Tucker has successfully delivered such a powerful message across with her brilliant writing that will make you laugh, smile and cry all in one go.</b> Well-written characters all around and enough depth to let you understand what drives their emotions &amp; actions.<br><br>If you can handle the rollercoaster of emotions and is able to ignore the spoiler-ish content above, <b>I highly recommend it because this book is a winner, in terms of writing and the emotional punch <s>and driving you insanely nuts.</s></b> <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>”Life’s all about trial and error.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="9612863892881886337" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
